yasmiñ'ca kho, bhikkhave, samaye līnaṃ cittaṃ hoti, kālo tasmiṃ samaye dhammavicayasambojjh'aṅgassa bhāvanāya, kālo vīriyasambojjh'aṅgassa bhāvanāya, kālo pītisambojjh'aṅgassa bhāvanāya.

dhorayho vata, bho, samaṇo gotamo, dhorayhavatā ca samuppannā sārīrikā vedanā dukkhā tibbā kharā kaṭukā asātā amanāpā sato sampajāno adhivāseti avihaññamāno'ti.

SN 1.38 sakalikasuttaṃ
dhorayhasīla

adj. virtuous; enduring; patient; lit. yoke carrying nature [dhorayha + sīla] ✓

Grammar adj, comp
Meaning virtuous; enduring; patient; lit. yoke carrying nature
Construction dhorayha + sīla
Compound kammadhāraya (dhorayha + sīla)
Commentary (DHPa) dhuravahanasīlatāya dhorayhasīlaṃ
Sanskrit dhaureya + śīla

tasmā hi
dhīrañ'ca paññañ'ca bahussutañ'ca,
dhorayhasīlaṃ vatavantam'ariyaṃ,
taṃ t'ādisaṃ sappurisaṃ sumedhaṃ,
bhajetha nakkhattapathaṃ'va candimā.

DHP 208 sukhavaggo
dhovati

pr. (+acc) washes; cleans; rinses [√dhov + a + ti] ✓

Grammar pr, trans (+acc)
Meaning washes; cleans; rinses
Root Family √dhov
Root √dhov･1 a (wash, rinse)
Base √dhov + a > dhova
Construction dhova + ti
Synonym sandhovati
Commentary (ANa) dhovatī'ti vikkhāleti.
Sanskrit dhāvati
Sanskrit Root √dhāv 1 (rinse)

santi, bhikkhave, jātarūpassa oḷārikā upakkilesā paṃsuvālukā sakkharakaṭhalā. tam'enaṃ paṃsudhovako vā paṃsudhovak'antevāsī vā doṇiyaṃ ākiritvā dhovati sandhovati niddhovati.

AN 3.102 paṃsudhovakasuttaṃ

kālena kālañ'ca vaṇaṃ dhoveyyāsi, kālena kālaṃ vaṇamukhaṃ ālimpeyyāsi, mā te na kālena kālaṃ vaṇaṃ dhovato na kālena kālaṃ vaṇamukhaṃ ālimpato pubbalohitaṃ vaṇamukhaṃ pariyonandhi.

MN 105 sunakkhattasuttaṃ
dhovana 1

nt. washing; cleaning; rinsing [√dhov + ana] ✓

Grammar nt, act, from dhovati
Meaning washing; cleaning; rinsing
Root Family √dhov
Root √dhov･1 a (wash, rinse)
Construction √dhov + ana
Derivative kita (ana)
Sanskrit dhāvana, dhovana (bsk)
Sanskrit Root √dhāv 1 (rinse)

tasmā hi ne namasseyya,
sakkareyya ca paṇḍito,
annena atha pānena,
vatthena sayanena ca,
ucchādanena nhāpanena,
pādānaṃ dhovanena ca.

AN 4.63 brahmasuttaṃ

atthi, bhikkhave, dakkhiṇesu janapadesu dhovanaṃ nāma. tattha hoti annam'pi pānam'pi khajjam'pi bhojjam'pi leyyam'pi peyyam'pi naccam'pi gītam'pi vāditam'pi. atth'etaṃ, bhikkhave, dhovanaṃ, n'etaṃ n'atthī'ti vadāmi.
